Salah — Prayer
intermediate
7 min
Conditions of the Jumu'ah Khutbah
States conditions for valid khutbah with proof and dispute

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to list the five or six conditions of the Jumu'ah khutbah according to the Hanafi school and explain the evidence for why it must precede the prayer.

Core Idea
The khutbah must precede the prayer, be intended, timely, with a listener, and uninterrupted — or Jumu'ah is invalid.

The Jumu'ah khutbah is a cornerstone of Friday worship. This passage from the Hashiya al-Tahtawi clarifies its essential conditions and the historical shift that established them. Mastering these conditions ensures the Jumu'ah prayer is performed validly according to the Hanafi school.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and its ruling
The khutbah is a condition (shart) for the validity of Jumu'ah. It is wajib, and if omitted, the Jumu'ah prayer is invalid.
The khutbah is not a pillar of the prayer itself but a prerequisite.
2
Locate the dalil
Find the mursal hadith from Abu Dawud that recounts the change from khutbah-after-prayer to khutbah-before-prayer.
This hadith is the primary proof for the condition of precedence.
3
Trace the wajh al-dalalah
The hadith shows that the Prophet changed the order after the revelation of Quran 62:11, establishing the khutbah before the prayer as a binding practice.
The change indicates a condition (shart) must precede its object.
4
Note the ikhtilaf
There is an intra-Hanafi disagreement on whether a listener is required. One narration says no listener is needed; the correct view (sahih) requires at least one qualified person.
Also, the Imamiyyah (Shi'a) reject the khutbah as a condition altogether.
5
Evaluate the Hanafi tarjih
The text states 'in the correct view' (fi al-sahih), adopting the requirement of at least one listener. This is the mufta bihi position.
The presence of a listener aligns with the purpose of a sermon.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
قوله : (والرابع الخطبة) فعلة بمعنى مفعولة فهي اسم لما يخطب به عناية من الخطب وهو في الأصل كلام بين اثنين قهستاني عن الأزاهر وهي بالضم في الموعظة، والجمع خطب، وبالكسر طلب التزوّج، والفعل فيهما كقتل وهي شرط بالإجماع خلافاً للإمامية وقد شذوا. قوله: (قبلها) أي قبل الصلاة لأنها شرطها، وشرط الشيء سابق عليه، وقد كانت الخطبة في صدر الإسلام بعد الصلاة كخطبة العيد، ثم نسخ وجعلت قبلها ففي مراسيل أبي داود كان رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم يصلي الجمعة قبل الخطبة حتى إذا كان ذات يوم، وهو يخطب وقد صلى الجمعة فدخل رجل فقال : إن دحية قد قدم وكان إذا قدم تلقوه بالدفاف فخرج الناس لم يظنوا إلا أنه لا شيء في ترك الخطبة، فأنزل الله تعالى الآية: (وإذا رأوا تجارة أو لهوا انفضوا إليها) [الجمعة/ ٦٢] فقدم النبي صلى الله عليه وسلم الخطبة الجمعة، وأخر الصلاة كذا في الشرح قوله: (محمد) لعطاسه) تعجباً. قوله : (لا) ينوب عن الخطبة هو أحد قولين والثاني أنه لا يشترط فيها القصد، وتقدم ما يفيده، وذكره صاحب صاحب التنوير في الذبائح. قوله: (في وقتها) فلو خطب قبله، وصلى فيه لا تصح لأنه من جملة الخصوصيات المقيدة بها حلبي. قوله: (لا عبي) بالجر عطفاً على قوله عبد الخ أي لا يكفي حضور صبي . ولا يشترط سماع جماعة فتصح الخطبة (ولو) كان الحاضر (واحداً) وروي عن الإمام وصاحبيه صحتها وإن لم يحضره أحد و (في) الرواية الثانية عنهم يشترط حضور واحد في (الصحيح) ويشترط أن لا يفصل بين الخطبة والصلاة بأكل وعمل قاطع، واختلف في صحتها لو ذهب لمنزله لغسل، أو وضوء فهذه خمس شروط، أو ست لصحة الخطبة فليتنبه لها
His saying: (and the fourth is the khutbah) — a verbal noun meaning that which is spoken with care; originally it is speech between two. Al-Qahistani from al-Azahir: it is with damm in the sense of sermon, plural khutab; with kasr it means marriage proposal. The verb in both is like qatala. It is a condition by consensus, contrary to the Imamiyyah who deviated. His saying: (before it) meaning before the prayer because it is its condition, and the condition of a thing precedes it. The khutbah in early Islam was after the prayer like the Eid khutbah, then it was abrogated and placed before. In the mursal of Abu Dawud: the Prophet used to pray Jumu'ah before the khutbah until one day, while he was delivering the khutbah after praying, a man entered and said: Dihyah has arrived and he used to be received with beating of drums, so the people left, thinking that there was no harm in leaving the khutbah. So Allah revealed the verse: 'And when they see a transaction or amusement, they rush to it' (62:11). So the Prophet put the khutbah before the prayer and delayed the prayer. His saying: (Muhammad sneezed) in wonder. His saying: (does not) substitute for the khutbah is one of two sayings; the second is that intention is not required in it. His saying: (in its time) if he gave the khutbah before it and prayed in it, it is not valid because it is among the specificities restricted to it. His saying: (not a boy) with jarr as a conjunction to his saying 'a slave', i.e., the presence of a boy is not sufficient. And it is not required that a congregation hears, so the khutbah is valid even if only one is present. And it is narrated from the Imam and his two companions that it is valid even if no one is present. In the second narration from them, the presence of one is required in the correct view. And it is required that there be no separation between the khutbah and the prayer by eating or an interrupting action. And there is disagreement on its validity if he goes to his home to wash or perform wudu. So these are five or six conditions for the validity of the khutbah, so be mindful of them.
Source pages p. 509

Commentary
This passage is a critical refinement (hashiya) detailing the conditions of the Jumu'ah khutbah. The fourth condition of Jumu'ah is the khutbah, which is a consensus of the Muslims except the Shi'a (Imamiyyah). The commentator provides linguistic analysis and then lists the conditions: 1) It must be before the prayer (originally it was after, but was abrogated by the incident of Dihyah when people left). 2) It must be performed with the intention (qasd) of the khutbah; a sneeze thanking Allah does not count. 3) It must be performed within the time of Jumu'ah. 4) Presence of at least one person from those upon whom Jumu'ah is obligated (a free, resident, adult male); a minor is not sufficient. There is an intra-Hanafi dispute: according to one narration, even one listener is not required; according to the correct view, at least one is required. 5) No separating action between the khutbah and the prayer, such as eating or a lengthy interruption. If one goes to perform wudu, there is disagreement. The final enumeration lists five or six conditions, depending on whether intention is counted separately.

Key Terms
الخطبة (al-khutbah): The sermon delivered before the Jumu'ah prayer; it is a condition for the validity of Jumu'ah.
قصد (qasd): Intent; the khutbah must be performed with the intention of being a khutbah, otherwise incidental speech does not count.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the correct Hanafi view, how many people must be present for the Jumu'ah khutbah?
A) At least forty.
B) At least one qualified person.
C) At least two.
D) None; it is valid even if no one is present.

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school requires the khutbah to be before the prayer, with intention, within its time, and with at least one qualified listener absent any interrupting action.
